// MOB_ID,Dummy skill and monster name,STATE,SKILL_ID,SKILL_LV,rate,casttime,delay,can stop the target,Condition,Condition value,Value 1,Value 2,Value 3,Value 4,Value 5,Emotion associate with the skill
// Dummy skill and monster name : when you can see the skill and mob name isn't it good?
//
// STATE: any At any time / idle Idle/standing / walk Walking / attack Attacking /
//        dead Dead / loot Loot / chase Following or pursuiting / Attacking back(?)
//        command
//
// Target: target Attacking PC / self Self / friend Friend
//	  around  surrounding (81 surrounding tails = around4)
//	  around1  9 surrounding tails of the caster (3*3)
//	  around2 25 surrounding tails of the caster (5*5)
//	  around3 49 surrounding tails of the caster (7*7)
//	  around4 81 surrounding tails of the caster (9*9)
//	  around5  9 surrounding tails of the target (3*3)
//	  around6 25 surrounding tails of the target (5*5)
//	  around7 49 surrounding tails of the target (7*7)
//	  around8 81 surrounding tails of the target (9*9)
//	  master / command / modechange
//	You can only use around for area of effect skills. You can only use friend if there is friends nearby.
//
// Condition: (Condition type)		(Specified condition value)
//	always             No condition
//	myhpltmaxrate      When caster max HP is under the specified %
//	mystatuson         When caster has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	mystatusoff        When caster has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	friendhpltmaxrate  When friend max HP is under the specified %
//	friendstatuson     When friend has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	friendstatusoff    When friend has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	attackpcgt         When attacking PC become more than the specified number
//	attackpcge         When attacking PC become equal or more than the specified number
//	slavelt            When the number of slave become less than the specified number
//	slavele            When the number of slave become equal or less than the specified number
//	closedattacked     When it is attacked in close range
//	longrangeattacked  When it is attacked by long range attacks
//	skillused          When it is attacked by a specified skill
//	casttargeted       When it is attacked by a skill with an area of effect
//	targethpgtmaxrate  When target max HP is over the specified %
//	targethpltmaxrate  When target max HP is under the specified %
//	targetstatuson     When target has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	targetstatusoff    When target has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	targethpgt         When target max HP is over the specified value
//	targethplt         When target max HP is under the specified value
//	masterhpgtmaxrate  When master max HP is over the specified value
//	masterhpltmaxrate  When master max HP is under the specified value
//	masterstatuson     When master has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	masterstatusoff    When master has an abnormal status (condition value)
//	rudeattacked       
//
//	The caracter status can be specified with the statuson/statusoff system
//	anybad     Which one of the 9 following abnormal status is it?
//	stone      Stone Cursed»	<- anybad correspondence
//	freeze     Frozen
//	stan       Stuned
//	sleep      Asleep
//	poison     Poisoned
//	curse      Cursed
//	silence    Silenced
//	confusion  Chaosed
//	blind      Blind	<- anybad correspondence
//	hiding     Hidden
//	sight      Using Sight
//	stone      Stone Cursed»(beeing completly stone cursed/pertified)
//	lexaeterna State of LA
// end of TN -----------------------------------------------------
